It is really difficult to come down from Huangshan Mountain. Tourists with leg pain, middle-aged and elderly tourists should choose more carefully. There are "Beware of Stairs" warning stickers posted everywhere on the hotel floor (as shown in the picture). The one square meter area of â€‹â€‹an elevator is full of bumps on all sides. When you enter the door, the ground is a large brick sculpture. It is lumpy even if you pull your luggage, up and down. It's extremely inconvenient, and the designer doesn't know what to think.
On the surface, the hotel's hardware facilities look very cultural, with collected bottles and cans everywhere, but in fact it is inconvenient for guests. As soon as they entered the door, they heard a teacher from a student tour group telling students to stay away. I'm afraid I'll have to pay for it if it gets damaged. The water in the garden should be beautiful, but it is neglected to keep the water turbid. The room facing the street was originally a landscape room with a river view, but the sound insulation of the windows was very poor, and the sealing of the sliding windows was very poor. It felt like sleeping on the side of the road. The sealing *****s in the bathroom also leaked as soon as they were washed. Many areas that should be improved were not improved. Instead, a lot of superficial effort was used.
Letâ€™s talk about service. The front desk system crashed and registration was impossible. The package booked by Ctrip included an airport drop-off service, but it was not included in the system. The hotel was obviously understaffed and service efficiency was greatly affected. The restaurant was also understaffed. When I went there at 8:30 in the morning, all kinds of dishes were out of stock, and the kitchen was slow to bring out supplies. By the way, the tables and chairs in the restaurant are not matching. The table is short and the chairs are high. You can only bend down to eat. I donâ€™t know where I found the dining table and chairs.
Fortunately, although the waiters are all uncles and aunts, they all smile and are very focused on their work. It can be seen that they want to serve customers well and cherish this job. But if the boss can give them more professional training and If we add more manpower, we won't make them so passive and hardworking.
It is estimated that the epidemic has indeed had an impact on the hotel industry, but other hotels we visited during our trip to Huangshan will be more attentive to improving service quality to win valuable customers, but this boss is obviously not very attentive.
Also, this is the only hotel I have ever seen where no one wears a mask. I was so scared that I quickly covered my mask tightly.
Having said all that, I really feel that this hotel is a pity. It can be seen that the owner is very rich and has invested a lot of money in the hotel. But after all, the hotel is for guests, and it also needs to be professional and put the guest experience first. That's the way to survive.
